# (PART\*) Supper {-}






# Data Visualization
Data visualization is a critical component to data analytics. Telling a story with data is becoming an increasingly important part of data analytics, a desired skill for all areas within the field. Creating, modifying, and customizing data visualizations will be covered within this section.

> *Visualization gives you answers to questions you didnâ€™t know you had <br> Ben Schneiderman*


## Creating plots
Visualizing data is an essential part of data analytics, either during data exploration or to convey findings of the analysis. There are many different plot types, the following are common plots used to visualize numeric and character data.


### Create a bar plot

```{=html}
  <thead class="gt_col_headings">
    <tr>
      <th class="gt_col_heading gt_columns_bottom_border gt_center" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><strong>Package</strong></th>
      <th class="gt_col_heading gt_columns_bottom_border gt_center" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><strong>Data</strong></th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody class="gt_table_body">
    <tr><td class="gt_row gt_center"><div class='gt_from_md'><p>readr<br>dplyr<br>ggplot2</p>
</div></td>
<td class="gt_row gt_center"><div class='gt_from_md'><p>sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv</p>
</div></td></tr>
  </tbody>
  
  
</table>
</div>
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("C:/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv") %>%
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(construction_grade))
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name) +
  geom_bar()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = construction_grade) +
  geom_bar()
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("C:/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name) +
  geom_histogram()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms) +
  geom_histogram()
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("C:/data/sample_parcel_assessed_value.csv") %>%
  dplyr::group_by(tax_year) %>%
  dplyr::tally() %>%
  dplyr::ungroup()
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2) +
  geom_line()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = tax_year, y = n) +
  geom_line()
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("C:/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2) +
  geom_point()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms) +
  geom_point()
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("C:/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2) +
  geom_boxplot()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = construction_grade, y = bedrooms) +
  geom_boxplot()
```


## Visualizing dimensions
Adding dimensions to the mix when visualizing provides deeper potential insights. Dimensions are typically used to change the colour or size of a plot's geometry.

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv") %>%
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(construction_grade))
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name) +
  geom_bar(fill = "hex colour")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = construction_grade) +
  geom_bar(fill = "#484848")
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2) +
  geom_point(color = "hex colour")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms) +
  geom_point(colour = "#484848")
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv") %>%
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(construction_grade))
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, fill = column_name2) +
  geom_bar()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = construction_grade, fill = garage) +
  geom_bar()
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point()
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, size = column_name3) +
  geom_point()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, size = bathrooms) +
  geom_point()
```


## Add text to a plot
Text provides context helping users understand the purpose and specific details related to the plot.

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("~/Github/r-recipe-book/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv") %>%
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(construction_grade))
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(title = "text")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(title = "Relationship of Bedrooms to Bathrooms")
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(subtitle = "text")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(subtitle = "Three HRM Neighbourboods")
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(x = "text")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(x = "Bedrooms")
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(y = "text")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(y = "Bathrooms")
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(caption = "text")
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  labs(caption = "Created with ggplot2")
```


## Customizing a plot
ggplot2 will generate acceptable plots with the default settings for many situations; data exploration, internal communication, but in many circumstances you will want to change the defaults to meet specific design needs. Customizing the look and style of a data visualization is essential to make your plot standout and grab the user's attention. 


### Add theme to a plot

```{=html}
<div id="tdbdnoufzy" style="overflow-x:auto;overflow-y:auto;width:auto;height:auto;">

  font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, 'Helvetica Neue', 'Fira Sans', 'Droid Sans', Arial, sans-serif;
}
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme_minimal()
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme_minimal()
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.major.x = element_blank(),
    panel.grid.major.y = element_blank()
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.major.x = element_blank(),
    panel.grid.major.y = element_blank()
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = element_blank(),
    panel.grid.minor.y = element_blank()
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = element_blank(),
    panel.grid.minor.y = element_blank()
  )
```


### Change major x/y grid line (colour/type/size)

```{=html}
<div id="vewfkyzovu" style="overflow-x:auto;overflow-y:auto;width:auto;height:auto;">
<style>html {
  font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, 'Helvetica Neue', 'Fira Sans', 'Droid Sans', Arial, sans-serif;
}

#vewfkyzovu .gt_table {
  display: table;
  border-collapse: collapse;
  margin-left: auto;
  margin-right: auto;
  color: #333333;
  font-size: 16px;
  font-weight: normal;
  font-style: normal;
  background-color: #FFFFFF;
  width: auto;
  border-top-style: solid;
```

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.major.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number),
    panel.grid.major.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number)
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.major.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.3),
    panel.grid.major.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.3)
  )
```

```{=html}
  font-size: 65%;

  <colgroup>
```

```{=html}
    <col style="width:350px;"/>
  </colgroup>
  <thead class="gt_header">

    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody class="gt_table_body">
    <tr><td class="gt_row gt_center"><div class='gt_from_md'><p>readr<br>dplyr<br>ggplot2</p>
</div></td>

</div></td></tr>
  </tbody>
  
  
</table>
</div>
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number)
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.1),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.1)
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    theme.position = "location"
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    theme.position = "bottom"
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    theme.position = "value"
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    theme.position = "none"
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number)
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.1),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.1)
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "type", size = number)
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.1),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "solid", size = 0.1)
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor.x = element_blank(),
    panel.grid.minor.y = element_blank()
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    axis.text.x = element_blank(),
    axis.text.y = element_blank()
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv")
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    axis.text.x = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number),
    axis.text.y = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number)
  )
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = bedrooms, y = bathrooms, color = bathrooms) +
  geom_point() +
  theme(
    axis.text.x = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 8),
    axis.text.y = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 8)
  )
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("~/Github/r-recipe-book/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv") %>%
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(construction_grade))
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_point() +
  scale_x_discrete(labels = function(x) str_wrap(x, width = number))
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
 df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = construction_grade) +
  geom_bar(fill = "#1E6E6E") +
  scale_x_discrete(labels = function(x) str_wrap(x, width = 10))
```

</br>

**Preparation**

```r
df <- readr::read_csv("~/Github/r-recipe-book/data/sample_dwelling_characteristics.csv") %>%
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(construction_grade))
```

</br>

**Sample Instructions**

```r
data %>%
  package::function() +
  aes(x = column_name1, y = column_name2, colour = column_name3) +
  geom_bar(fill = "hex colour") +
  labs(title = "text",
       subtitle = "text",
       x = "text",
       y = "text",
       caption = "text") +
  theme(
    # Text -- title, subtitle, labels, and caption
    plot.title = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number, face = "text"),
    plot.subtitle = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number),
    plot.caption = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number),
    axis.text.x = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number),
    axis.text.y = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "hex colour", size = number),
    
    # Chart elements -- grids
    panel.grid.major.x = ggplot2::element_blank(),
    panel.grid.major.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "hex colour", linetype = "text", size = number),
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_blank(),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_blank(),
    panel.background = element_blank()
  ) +
  scale_x_discrete(labels = function(x) str_wrap(x, width = number))
```

</br>

**Actual Instructions**

```r
df %>%
  ggplot2::ggplot() +
  aes(x = construction_grade) +
  geom_bar(fill = "#1E6E6E") +
  labs(title = "Distribution of Housing Construction Grade",
       subtitle = "Three HRM Neighbourboods",
       x = "Construction Grade",
       y = "Number of Houses",
       caption = "Create with ggplot2") +
  theme(
    # Text -- title, subtitle, labels, and caption
    plot.title = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 14, face = "bold"),
    plot.subtitle = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 12),
    plot.caption = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 6),
    axis.text.x = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 8),
    axis.text.y = ggplot2::element_text(colour = "#484848", size = 8),
    
    # Chart elements -- grids
    panel.grid.major.x = ggplot2::element_blank(),
    panel.grid.major.y = ggplot2::element_line(colour = "#484848", linetype = "dotted", size = 0.2),
    panel.grid.minor.x = ggplot2::element_blank(),
    panel.grid.minor.y = ggplot2::element_blank(),
    panel.background = element_blank()
  ) +
  scale_x_discrete(labels = function(x) str_wrap(x, width = 10))
```
